OK: 0 rows affected

OK: 0 rows affected

OK: 0 rows affected
--- STMT 8 ---
SQL: SET TimeZone = 'UTC'
OK: 0 rows affected
--- STMT 9 ---
SQL: SELECT current_schema() AS current_schema, current_setting('TimeZone') AS timezone, current_setting('DateStyle') AS datestyle, current_setting('IntervalStyle') AS intervalstyle
RESULT: 4 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: current_schema, timezone, datestyle, intervalstyle
ROW: compat | UTC | ISO, YMD | postgres
--- STMT 10 ---
SQL: SELECT version()
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: version
ROW: PostgreSQL 18.0
--- STMT 11 ---
SQL: SELECT 1 AS i, 1.5 AS n, 'x'::text AS t, TRUE AS b, NULL AS z
RESULT: 5 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: i, n, t, b, z
ROW: 1 | 1.5 | x | t | NULL
--- STMT 12 ---
SQL: SELECT pg_typeof(1), pg_typeof(1.5), pg_typeof('x'::text), pg_typeof(TRUE), pg_typeof(NULL)
RESULT: 5 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: pg_typeof, pg_typeof, pg_typeof, pg_typeof, pg_typeof
ROW: integer | numeric | text | boolean | unknown
--- STMT 13 ---
SQL: CREATE TABLE t(a int)
OK: 0 rows affected
--- STMT 14 ---
SQL: CREATE TABLE t(a int)
ERROR [42P07]: ERROR: relation "t" already exists

SQL: SELECT * FROM

--- STMT 17 ---
SQL: DROP SCHEMA compat CASCADE
OK: 0 rows affected

OK: 0 rows affected
--- STMT 9 ---
SQL: SELECT current_schema() AS current_schema, current_setting('TimeZone') AS timezone, current_setting('DateStyle') AS datestyle, current_setting('IntervalStyle') AS intervalstyle
RESULT: 4 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: current_schema, timezone, datestyle, intervalstyle
ROW: compat | UTC | ISO, YMD | postgres
--- STMT 10 ---
SQL: CREATE TABLE ftab(a int, b int, c text)
OK: 0 rows affected
--- STMT 11 ---
SQL: INSERT INTO ftab VALUES (1,10,'x'), (2,20,'y'), (3,NULL,'x'), (NULL,40,NULL)
OK: 4 rows affected
--- STMT 12 ---
SQL: CREATE FUNCTION addxy(x int, y int DEFAULT 100) RETURNS int LANGUAGE SQL AS $$ SELECT x + y $$
OK: 0 rows affected
--- STMT 13 ---
SQL: CREATE FUNCTION namedemo(a int, b text DEFAULT 'zzz', c boolean DEFAULT false) RETURNS text LANGUAGE SQL AS $$ SELECT a::text || ':' || b || ':' || c::text $$
OK: 0 rows affected
--- STMT 14 ---
SQL: -- ordinary and positional calls SELECT addxy(1,2), addxy(1)
RESULT: 2 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: addxy, addxy
ROW: 3 | 101
--- STMT 15 ---
SQL: SELECT substring('abcdef' FROM 2 FOR 3)
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: substring
ROW: bcd
--- STMT 16 ---
SQL: SELECT overlay('Txxxxas' placing 'hom' from 2 for 4)
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: overlay
ROW: Thomas
--- STMT 17 ---
SQL: -- named and mixed notation SELECT namedemo(a => 5, b => 'qq', c => true)
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: namedemo
ROW: 5:qq:true
--- STMT 18 ---
SQL: SELECT namedemo(c => true, a => 5, b => 'qq')
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: namedemo
ROW: 5:qq:true
--- STMT 19 ---
SQL: SELECT namedemo(5, c => true)
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: namedemo
ROW: 5:zzz:true
--- STMT 20 ---
SQL: SELECT namedemo(5, 'bb')
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: namedemo
ROW: 5:bb:false
--- STMT 21 ---
SQL: SELECT addxy(y => 7, x => 8)
RESULT: 1 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: addxy
ROW: 15
--- STMT 22 ---
SQL: -- aggregates SELECT count(*), count(a), sum(a), avg(a), min(c), max(c) FROM ftab
RESULT: 6 columns, 1 rows
COLUMNS: count, count, sum, avg, min, max
